  • a) Commission Contract In English click here

    b) Contract De Comision În Română click aici
  • a) All Contracts signed but not paid by our clients
    - no contract yet

    b) All Contracts that clients sent payment in advance and ongoing
    - no contract yet

    c) All Contracts completed
    - no contract yet
  • We only buy product from suppliers for clients at their demand ( We don't store products if not requested by client company, we try to save energy and lower cost )

    Step 1 You can read the commision contract to understand it
    https://www.docdroid.net/eqpwaTm/commision-contract-the-principal-reads-fills-his-part-of-the-contract-and-sends-back-to-blue-sea-export-import-srl-email-pdf
    "5.2 The client has the right to inspect, test the quality of the goods described in Appendix no. 1 at the time of delivery and to reject them if they are not in accordance with the contractual clauses."

    Step 2 After we verify your documents and you check our documents, we get exclusive rights agreement and you also sign the declaration of compliance if you wish to become our supplier

    Step 3 We contact the client companies or they view your catalog and public documents you sent us on www.blueseaexportimport.com or social media ---> to show that product(s) is safe, respects environmental, human and animal rights legislation, that it's transparent and traceable and that your an authorised producer / transporter or other service provider ( client company buys what it wants, could be another product from another supplier )

    Step 4 You send sample(s) to client(s) companies ( we pay you sample and transport cost, the company client will pay for it when it requests sample )

    Step 5 If the client company likes the product(s), the client signs a commission contract with BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. ( we send you a copy also to read )

    Step 6 If we all agree, the client company(s) sends payment in advance 100% to BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. after the invoice is generated.

    Step 7 BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. send you the producer-manufacturer-merchant-trader / transporter / logistics or anyone how is part of the supply chain a copy of bank statement proof that payment is in our account

    Step 8 You ship product to each client depending on demand
    ( example
    --- client A 3 tones small factory in country x
    --- client B 10 tones supermarket chain in country y
    --- client C 50 tones big processing factory in country z )

    Step 9 Client(s) inspect the product(s) if according to Appendix I of commission contract and after client signs the handover receipt we send you the full payment to your bank account or if product not ok and not according to contract it is send to you back at your own cost or compost centers or recycling center.
  • *Note you have to be very transparent / honest with documents you send else we can not export-import your products and we will refuse exclusive rights partnership.
    If you wish to become our supplier please send to our email blueseaexportimport [at] gmail.com ( you must be the CEO of the company ) the documents requested bellow:

    PART I PROOF THAT YOU ARE A PROFESSIONAL

    A. PDF Scanned Copy of your company business license
    B. PDF Scanned Copy Useful documents to show customs and client companies ( example ISO 9001 certificate )
    C. PDF Scanned Copy of weight verified scale / balance / sensor by your country metrologic institution where applicable ( when you sell by kg / tone , proof you the seller don't cheat clients at weighing scale )
    D. Photos and videos of product(s), labels , packaging, trays, crates, boxes, pallets, clean storage space, workers and workplace
    E. Let us know in what language you can translate the labels and documents ( some countries want documents and labels translated when doing export - import formalities )

    PART II SAFETY AND ENVIRONMENT DOCUMENTS

    A. If you manufacture or if transport Food Products ( Food Operators ):
    ++++ PDF Scanned Copy of HACCP or ISO 22000 for ( Manufacturing - Packhouses and Proccesing Factories ) / Handling / Transport
    ++++ PDF Scanned Copy of Food Safety Certificate issued by your Country Government ( Examples of food safety organisations: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_food_safety_organisations )

    B. If you manufacture Food Products or Non-food Products:

  • BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. Frequently Asked Questions

    If your the CEO of the supplier company read all the info on our website.

    Why does BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. needs exclusive rights agreement from supplier partners ?

    Answer: We need the agreement do to fact some clients and competitors try to steal our suppliers, that we work hard to find (it costs time to find good suppliers)

    What is the Declaration of compliance , why does your company CEO needs to sign it ?

    Answer: In some countries some people don't respect human and animal rights , environment laws , they put counterfeit products and carcinogenic plastic on the market, they are corrupt. It's a promise your company respects common sense laws and that your a good company.

    Do i have to pay BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. any money to become a supplier - partner?

    Answer: NO, we don't take any money from you, the client company pays us 30% commission, you must send us proof you are a legal company and that you have all the documents to add you in our list of suppliers.

    If i am exclusive rights supplier-partner will BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. buy for their clients only from me ?

    Answer: No, we buy only from supplier-partners that signed the exclusive agreement, that have the best offer and the best price and that client wants. Just like in a supermarket we sign agreements with suppliers - partners and client company picks product he wants from catalog

    Is it possible to run away with clients 100% advance payment or to scam the clients or suppliers ?

    Answer: No because the money is traceable, it is all done electronic via bank transfer, it can be easy traced. For large amounts of money, banks request all documents before you can deposit, send or withdraw. There are security measures to prevent bad things. Company bank accounts are not like personal bank accounts or cash. You can use them for company needs only.

    If i am a supplier - partner can i get my money in cash ?

    Answer: No , you will get your money via bank transfer only after client inspects the product(s) on arrival and after he signs over the handover receipt. If products are not like in commission contract either transporter did not transport properly the products, you the supplier did not packaged properly the products or the products or not the same we agreed in exclusive rights contract. You will not get payed for damaged products or products that are not the same as in commission contract and exclusive rights agreement. All have to be traced for governments taxes and accounting reasons also.

    Can i get my money via letter of credit 30% in advance or via other method ?

    Answer: No , the commission contract is standard for all companies. We all get payed after client inspects product when it arrives at his location and after he signs handover receipt. BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. just escrows the electronic money for all parties until goods are delivered.

    Does BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. advertise my products ?

    Answer: No, we advertise BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. like a supermarket but B2B, your product will be in a catalog and people will buy it if they want it.

    Does BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. store and transport the products ?

    Answer: No, we aquire products for client companies only on demand, we store products only if they pay for this service and we hire transporters to transport the goods if client companies pay for this service.
    We don't store products just to have them on stock, and pay bills for things we don't need, we try to lower product(s) prices, buy quality products only on demand for clients and we try to reduce energy costs us and for our clients.
